            <script type="text/javascript">
             jQuery.noConflict();
        jQuery("#back2top").css("right",(document.body.clientWidth&gt;1072?((document.body.clientWidth-1062)/2):5)+"px");
        jQuery(document).ready(function(){
            if((document.body.scrollTop|document.documentElement.scrollTop)&lt;document.documentElement.clientHeight/4.0)
                jQuery('#back2top').hide();
            jQuery(window).scroll(function(){
                if((document.body.scrollTop|document.documentElement.scrollTop)&lt;document.documentElement.clientHeight/4.0){
                    jQuery('#back2top').fadeOut("slow", function(){jQuery('#back2top').hide();});
                }else{
                    jQuery('#back2top').fadeIn("slow");
                }
            });
        });
        jQuery(window).resize(function(){
            if (!((document.body.scrollTop | document.documentElement.scrollTop) &lt; document.documentElement.clientHeight / 4.0))
                jQuery("#back2top").css("right", (document.body.clientWidth &gt; 1072 ? ((document.body.clientWidth - 1062) / 2) : 5) + "px");
        });
        function screenscroll(){
            var i=80;
            var t=setInterval(function(){
                if(document.body.scrollTop&gt;=0)
                    document.body.scrollTop-=i;
                else
                    document.body.scrollTop=0;
                if(document.documentElement.scrollTop&gt;=0)
                    document.documentElement.scrollTop-=i;
                else document.documentElement.scrollTop=0;
                if(i&gt;10)i--;
                if((document.body.scrollTop|document.documentElement.scrollTop)==0)
                    window.clearInterval(t);
            },1);
        }

              <script type="text/javascript">
               function expandcontent(cid,object){
        var len=document.getElementById("all_view").childNodes.length;
        for(var i=0;i&lt;len;i++){
            document.getElementById("all_view").childNodes.item(i).className="no_div";
        }
        document.getElementById(cid).className="display_div";
        var lenli=document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.length;
        for(var y=0;y&lt;lenli;y++){
            if(document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.item(y).nodeName=="LI"){
                document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.item(y).className='';
                document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.item(y).firstChild.className='';
            }

                   <script type="text/javascript">
                    //&lt;![CDATA[
var DateOption = Class.create({

    getDaysInMonth: function(month, year)
    {
        var curDate = new Date();
        if (!month) {
            month = curDate.getMonth();
        }
        if (2 == month &amp;&amp; !year) { // leap year assumption for unknown year
            return 29;
        }
        if (!year) {
            year = curDate.getFullYear();
        }
        return 32 - new Date(year, month - 1, 32).getDate();
    },

    reloadMonth: function(event)
    {
        var selectEl = event.findElement();
        var idParts = selectEl.id.split("_");
        if (idParts.length != 3) {
            return false;
        }
        var optionIdPrefix = idParts[0] + "_" + idParts[1];
        var month = parseInt($(optionIdPrefix + "_month").value);
        var year = parseInt($(optionIdPrefix + "_year").value);
        var dayEl = $(optionIdPrefix + "_day");

        var days = this.getDaysInMonth(month, year);

        //remove days
        for (var i = dayEl.options.length - 1; i &gt;= 0; i--) {
            if (dayEl.options[i].value &gt; days) {
                dayEl.remove(dayEl.options[i].index);
            }
        }

        // add days
        var lastDay = parseInt(dayEl.options[dayEl.options.length-1].value);
        for (i = lastDay + 1; i &lt;= days; i++) {
            this.addOption(dayEl, i, i);
        }
    },

    addOption: function(select, text, value)
    {
        var option = document.createElement('OPTION');
        option.value = value;
        option.text = text;

        if (select.options.add) {
            select.options.add(option);
        } else {
            select.appendChild(option);
        }
    }
});
dateOption = new DateOption();
//]]&gt;
                   </script>

        var optionFileUpload = {
            productForm : $('product_addtocart_form'),
            formAction : '',
            formElements : {},
            upload : function(element){
                this.formElements = this.productForm.select('input', 'select', 'textarea', 'button');
                this.removeRequire(element.readAttribute('id').sub('option_', ''));

                template = '&lt;iframe id="upload_target" name="upload_target" style="width:0; height:0; border:0;"&gt;&lt;\/iframe&gt;';

                Element.insert($('option_'+element.readAttribute('id').sub('option_', '')+'_uploaded_file'), {after: template});

                this.formAction = this.productForm.action;

                var baseUrl = 'http://www.alizeebridal.com/catalog/product/upload/';
                var urlExt = 'option_id/'+element.readAttribute('id').sub('option_', '');

                this.productForm.action = parseSidUrl(baseUrl, urlExt);
                this.productForm.target = 'upload_target';
                this.productForm.submit();
                this.productForm.target = '';
                this.productForm.action = this.formAction;
            },
            removeRequire : function(skipElementId){
                for(var i=0; i&lt;this.formElements.length; i++){
                    if (this.formElements[i].readAttribute('id') != 'option_'+skipElementId+'_file' &amp;&amp; this.formElements[i].type != 'button') {
                        this.formElements[i].disabled='disabled';
                    }
                }
            },

        Product.Options = Class.create();
        Product.Options.prototype = {
            initialize : function(config) {
                this.config = config;
                this.reloadPrice();
                document.observe("dom:loaded", this.reloadPrice.bind(this));
            },
            reloadPrice : function() {
                var config = this.config;
                var skipIds = [];
                $$('body .product-custom-option').each(function(element){
                    var optionId = 0;
                    element.name.sub(/[0-9]+/, function(match){
                        optionId = parseInt(match[0], 10);
                    });
                    if (config[optionId]) {
                        var configOptions = config[optionId];
                        var curConfig = {price: 0};
                        if (element.type == 'checkbox' || element.type == 'radio') {
                            if (element.checked) {
                                if (typeof configOptions[element.getValue()] != 'undefined') {
                                    curConfig = configOptions[element.getValue()];
                                }
                            }
                        } else if(element.hasClassName('datetime-picker') &amp;&amp; !skipIds.include(optionId)) {
                            dateSelected = true;
                            $$('.product-custom-option[id^="options_' + optionId + '"]').each(function(dt){
                                if (dt.getValue() == '') {
                                    dateSelected = false;
                                }
                            });
                            if (dateSelected) {
                                curConfig = configOptions;
                                skipIds[optionId] = optionId;
                            }
                        } else if(element.type == 'select-one' || element.type == 'select-multiple') {
                            if ('options' in element) {
                                $A(element.options).each(function(selectOption){
                                    if ('selected' in selectOption &amp;&amp; selectOption.selected) {
                                        if (typeof(configOptions[selectOption.value]) != 'undefined') {
                                            curConfig = configOptions[selectOption.value];
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                        } else {
                            if (element.getValue().strip() != '') {
                                curConfig = configOptions;
                            }
                        }
                        if(element.type == 'select-multiple' &amp;&amp; ('options' in element)) {
                            $A(element.options).each(function(selectOption) {
                                if (('selected' in selectOption) &amp;&amp; typeof(configOptions[selectOption.value]) != 'undefined') {
                                    if (selectOption.selected) {
                                        curConfig = configOptions[selectOption.value];
                                    } else {
                                        curConfig = {price: 0};
                                    }
                                    optionsPrice.addCustomPrices(optionId + '-' + selectOption.value, curConfig);
                                    optionsPrice.reload();
                                }
                            });
                        } else {
                            optionsPrice.addCustomPrices(element.id || optionId, curConfig);
                            optionsPrice.reload();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }
        function validateOptionsCallback(elmId, result) {
            var container = $(elmId).up('ul.options-list');
            if (result == 'failed') {
                container.removeClassName('validation-passed');
                container.addClassName('validation-failed');
            } else {
                container.removeClassName('validation-failed');
                container.addClassName('validation-passed');
            }
        }

                   <script type="text/javascript">
                    var j2t_points = 0;
    var j2t_options = 0;

    var j2t_product_id = 1928;
    document.observe("dom:loaded", function() {
        if ($('qty')){
            Event.observe($('qty'), 'change', function(){ $('j2t-pts').innerHTML = j2t_math_points($('qty').value, j2t_points); });
        }


        
        var product_settings   = $$('.super-attribute-select');
        if (product_settings.length &gt; 0){
                product_settings.each(function(element){
                Event.observe(element, 'change', function() {
                    if (element.value != ''){
                        j2t_points = json_credit[element.value];
                        $('j2t-pts').innerHTML = j2t_math_points($('qty').value, j2t_points);
                    }
                });
            });
            var json_credit = [];
        }
            });

    function j2t_math_points(qty, pts_changed){
        var val_return = 0;
        if (isNaN(parseFloat(qty))) {
            qty = 1;
        }
        if(qty &gt; 0){
            val_return = (pts_changed + j2t_options) * qty;
        } else if(pts_changed &gt; 0) {
            val_return = pts_changed + j2t_options;
        }
        
        return Math.ceil(val_return);
    }
                   </script>
                   <script type="text/javascript">
                    var json_option_credit = {"302840":{"1256098":0,"1256099":0,"1256100":0,"1256101":0,"1256102":0,"1256103":0,"1256104":0,"1256105":0,"1256106":0,"1256107":0,"1256108":0,"1256109":0,"1256110":0,"1256111":0,"1256112":0,"1256113":0,"1256114":0,"1256115":0,"1256116":0,"1256117":0,"1256118":0,"1256119":0,"1256120":0,"1256121":0,"1256122":0,"1256123":0,"1256124":0,"1256125":0,"1256126":0,"1256127":0,"1256128":0,"1256129":0,"1256130":0,"1256131":0,"1256132":0,"1256133":0,"1256134":0,"1256135":0,"1256136":0,"1256137":0},"302841":{"1256138":0,"1256139":0,"1256140":0,"1256141":0,"1256142":0,"1256143":0,"1256144":0,"1256145":0,"1256146":9,"1256147":9,"1256148":9,"1256149":19,"1256150":19,"1256151":19},"302848":{"1256152":19},"302839":{"1256095":0,"1256096":30,"1256097":60},"302842":0,"302843":0,"302844":0,"302845":0,"302846":0,"302847":0};

    document.observe("dom:loaded", function() {
        option_select   = $$('.product-custom-option');

        if (option_select.length &gt; 0){
            option_select.each(function(element){
                Event.observe(element, 'change', function() {
                    j2t_options = reloadCreditOption();
                    $('j2t-pts').innerHTML = j2t_math_points($('qty').value, j2t_points);
                });
            });
        }
    });

    

    function reloadCreditOption(){
        var optionPts = 0;


        


        config = json_option_credit;
        skipIds = [];
        $$('.product-custom-option').each(function(element){
            var optionId = 0;
            element.name.sub(/[0-9]+/, function(match){
                optionId = match[0];
            });
            if (config[optionId]) {
                if (element.type == 'checkbox' || element.type == 'radio') {
                    if (element.checked) {
                        if (config[optionId][element.getValue()]) {
                            optionPts += parseFloat(config[optionId][element.getValue()]);
                        }
                    }
                } else if(element.hasClassName('datetime-picker') &amp;&amp; !skipIds.include(optionId)) {
                    dateSelected = true;
                    $$('.product-custom-option[id^="options_' + optionId + '"]').each(function(dt){
                        if (dt.getValue() == '') {
                            dateSelected = false;
                        }
                    });
                    if (dateSelected) {
                        optionPts += parseFloat(config[optionId]);
                        skipIds[optionId] = optionId;
                    }
                } else if(element.type == 'select-one' || element.type == 'select-multiple') {
                    if (element.options) {
                        $A(element.options).each(function(selectOption){
                            if (selectOption.selected) {
                                if (config[optionId][selectOption.value]) {
                                    optionPts += parseFloat(config[optionId][selectOption.value]);
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                } else {
                    if (element.getValue().strip() != '') {
                        optionPts += parseFloat(config[optionId]);
                    }
                }
            }
        });

        
        return optionPts;
    }

jQuery('span.qty-btn').mouseout(function(){jQuery(this).removeClass("hover")});
function p_add(){
   //alert('adfadfasdfasdfsdf');
   var val=document.getElementById('qty');
   //alert(val.value);
   if(val.value&gt;=100){
    val.value=99;
   }
    val.value=parseInt(val.value)+1;
	//alert(val.value);

}
function p_sub(){
    var val=document.getElementById('qty');
if(val.value&lt;=1){
    val.value=2;
   }
    val.value=parseInt(val.value)-1;
	
}

	jQuery('.qty-btn-block').css('border-color','#FB5888');
	jQuery('.qty-btn-block span').css('border-color','#FB5888');
}

function qty_blur(){
	jQuery('.qty-btn-block').css('border-color','');
	jQuery('.qty-btn-block span').css('border-color','');
}

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 var selected = [];
            function calculate(price,num){
                //alert("fdfd");
                var product_price = parseFloat(price);
                var selectedid = parseInt(num);
                var all = parseFloat(document.getElementById("fitting-amount").innerHTML);
                var allprice = parseFloat(document.getElementById("fitting-price").innerHTML);
                if(in_array(selectedid,selected)){
                    selected.Remove(selectedid);
                    document.getElementById("fitting-amount").innerHTML = parseInt(all) - 1;
                    var Pri  = parseFloat(allprice) - parseFloat(product_price); 
                    document.getElementById("fitting-price").innerHTML = Pri.toFixed(2);
                }else{
                    document.getElementById("fitting-amount").innerHTML = parseInt(all) + 1;
                    var Pri = parseFloat(allprice) + parseFloat(product_price);
                    document.getElementById("fitting-price").innerHTML = Pri.toFixed(2); 
                    selected.push(selectedid)
                }
            }
            Array.prototype.Remove = function(val) {
                for(var i=0;i&lt;this.length;i++){
                    if(this[i]   ===   val)
                    {this.splice(i,1);}
                }
            } 
            function in_array(needle, haystack) {
                type = typeof needle
                if(type == "string" || type == "number") {
                    for(var i in haystack) {
                        if(haystack[i] == needle) {
                            return true;
                        }
                    }
                }
                return false;
            }
                </script>

                  <a id="shipping-methods" name="shipping-methods">
                  </a>
                  <p>
                   <span style="font-size: small;">
                    <strong>
                     Estimate Shipping Time
                    </strong>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Before your order is shipped, Alizeebridal.com has to process your order and put all your items through its strict qualitycontrol tests. Because of this,
                   <strong>
                    Total Delivery Time
                   </strong>
                   is different from shipping time alone.
                   <br/>
                   <strong>
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                    Total Delivery Time = Processing Time+ Shipping Time
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <img alt="" src="http://www.alizeebridal.com/media/wysiwyg/33.jpg"/>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                    Processing Time
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                   </strong>
                   The process time is
                   <strong>
                    8-15 days
                   </strong>
                   for Wedding Party, Special Occasion and
                   <strong>
                    15
                   </strong>
                   <strong>
                    -18 days
                   </strong>
                   for Wedding Dresses.
                   <strong>
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                    Shipping Time
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Expedited Shipping
                   <br/>
                   <strong>
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   This shipping method is the fastest available. Delivery times are between
                   <strong>
                    2
                   </strong>
                   <strong>
                    -6 days
                   </strong>
                   to all major destinations. Shipping costvary from different items.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Standard Shipping
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Standard shipping costs less but takes a bit longer than expedited shipping. Delivery times are between
                   <strong>
                    5-10 days
                   </strong>
                   to all major destinations.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                    The Statement for Urgent Orders
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   If you need your items urgently, please select Expedited Shipping (It's about 2-6 working days and not free on our website). Select your country as shipping destination, and then, pay for the shipping fee, so that we can ship out your items ASAP.
                  </p>

                   </strong>

                   </strong>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   We sell products that we believe to be of high quality and reliability. Before shipping each dress to our customers, our Q&amp;C personnel will do detailed check to ensure the high quality and Never on purpose send out damaged or faulty goods.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                    5.How is our store different from other online dress stores?
                   </strong>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   Our store goes right to the source to purchase our beautiful gowns. The gowns we sell are of the same high quality as the designers sold in traditional salons and by other online retailers. Although we do not sell designer labeled gowns, you still get a beautiful bridal gown, without the designer price.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <strong>
                    6.How much duty, customs tariffs, VAT and/or taxes are charged on international orders?
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <br/>
                   In some cases, your destination country may charge customs duties or other taxes. We have no control over these charges as customs policies vary widely from country to country. Please check with your local customs office for further information.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <br/>
                   <strong>
                    7. The dress price you wrote on the invoice is lower than the actual price,why?
                   </strong>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   For avoiding the custom tax,we always write a lower price on invoice so that the parcel can pass the custom without any extra. Otherwise, customers have to pay a high amount import custom tax.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   <br/>
                   <strong>
                    8. What is your Return Policy?
                   </strong>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>

If your product arrives in a defective manner, mis-shipped , you are qualified to get a full refund. However, if the item is not faulty or it is made in accordance with the size you ordered but does not fit, please note that we will NOT accept your returned item.

                var dialog = $('.review-dialog-block');
                var el = $('#review-form input');
                el.focus(function(){
                    dialog.css('height',dialog.height());
                    dialog.css('height','auto');
                })
                el.blur(function(){
                    dialog.css('height',dialog.height());
                    dialog.css('height','auto');
                })
            }

            Validation.addAllThese(
                    [
                        ['validate-rating', 'Please select one of each of the ratings above', function(v) {
                            var trs = $('product-review-table').select('tr');
                            var inputs;
                            var error = 1;

                            for( var j=0; j &lt; trs.length; j++ ) {
                                var tr = trs[j];
                                if( j &gt; 0 ) {
                                    inputs = tr.select('input');

                                    for( i in inputs ) {
                                        if( inputs[i].checked == true ) {
                                            error = 0;
                                        }
                                    }

                                    if( error == 1 ) {
                                        return false;
                                    } else {
                                        error = 1;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            return true;
                        }]
                    ]
            );
                        $(".overall-raiting ul li").mouseover(
                function(){
                    var tthis = this;
                    var $li = $(tthis).parent().children('li');
                    $li.removeClass('active');
                    $li.each(function(){
                        $(this).addClass('active');
                        if ( tthis == this ) return false;
                    })
                    $(this).find('input.radio').attr('checked',true);
                }
            );
        });
    })(DRjQuery)
    //]]&gt;
                   </script>

                function expandcontent(cid,object){
                var len=document.getElementById("all_view").childNodes.length;
                for(var i=0;i&lt;len;i++){
                    document.getElementById("all_view").childNodes.item(i).className="no_div";
                }
                document.getElementById(cid).className="display_div";
                var lenli=document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.length;
                for(var y=0;y&lt;lenli;y++){
                    if(document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.item(y).nodeName=="LI"){
                        document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.item(y).className='';
                        document.getElementById("viewli").childNodes.item(y).firstChild.className='';
                    }
                }
                object.className="view_a";
                object.parentNode.className="view_li";
